   <script type="text/javascript">
    function ResizeSaleHeaderImage()
		{
			var $Ctn = $J( '.contenthub_background_holder' );
			if ( $Ctn.length !== 0 )
			{
				var getBackgroundImageSize = function(el) {
					var imageUrl = $J(el).css('background-image').match(/^url\(["']?(.+?)["']?\)$/);
					var dfd = new $J.Deferred();

					if (imageUrl) {
						var image = new Image();
						image.onload = dfd.resolve;
						image.onerror = dfd.reject;
						image.src = imageUrl[1];
					} else {
						dfd.reject();
					}

					return dfd.then(function() {
						return { width: this.width, height: this.height };
					});
				};

				getBackgroundImageSize( $Ctn )
					.then( function ( takeoverImage ) {

						var k_nContentWidth = 940 + 32;
						var flTakeoverRatio = takeoverImage.width / k_nContentWidth;

						$J( window ).on( 'Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreHomeLayout', function ()
						{
							if ( window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode() )
							{
								$Ctn.css( 'background-position', 'center 0vw' );
								var bgSize = Math.max( Math.floor( 100 * flTakeoverRatio ), 180 );
								$Ctn.css( 'background-size', bgSize + '% auto' );
								var spacerHeight = Math.min( ( takeoverImage.height / k_nContentWidth * 100 ) * 1.2, 50 );
								$J( '.contenthub_takeover_sizer' ).css( 'height', spacerHeight  + 'vw' );
								$J( '.fullscreen-bg__video' ).css( 'height', spacerHeight  + 'vw' );
								$J( '.contenthub_page_background' ).css( 'background', 'none' );
							}
							else
							{
								$Ctn.css( 'top', '' ).css( 'background-position', '' ).css( 'background-size', '' );
								$J( '.fullscreen-bg__video' ).css( 'height', 0 );
								$J( '.contenthub_takeover_sizer' ).css( 'height', prevSizer );
								$J( '.contenthub_page_background' ).css( 'background', prevBackground );
							}
						} ).trigger( 'Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreHomeLayout' );
					} )
					.fail( function () {
						console.log( 'Could not get size because could not load image' );
					} );
			}
		}

		var prevSizer;
		var prevBackground;

		$J( document ).ready( function () {
			prevSizer =  $J( '.contenthub_takeover_sizer' ).css( 'height' );
			prevBackground = $J( '.contenthub_page_background' ).css( 'background' );
			ResizeSaleHeaderImage();
		});
   </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      $J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode =window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

					if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
						$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

					if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						$ResponsiveNavCtn.append( $Header );
					else
						$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


					if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
					{
						$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
						$Header.show();
						var nMenuHeight = $J('#store_header' ).height() + $J('#store_header' ).offset().top;
						if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nMenuHeight )
							$Window.scrollTop( nMenuHeight - GetResponsiveHeaderFixedOffsetAdjustment() );

						$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
					}
				} ).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu');

									if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
					{
						var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_241_4_coop', 'US', 1, 'english', g_rgUserPreferences, '10545030' );
					}
				

			} );
     </script>

       <script>
        GStoreItemData.AddNavParams( {
		"genre_large_cluster": "1_241_4_coop_201"	} );

	// populate_genre_large_cluster
	function populate_genre_large_cluster( rgClusterItems, fnReason )
	{

		function PopulateTemplate( strTemplate, rgArguments )
		{
			var out = strTemplate;

			for( var i=0; i< rgArguments.length; i++)
			{
				var replace = "%"+(i+1)+"\\$s";
				var re = new RegExp(replace,"g");
				out = out.replace(re, rgArguments[i]);
			}

			return out;
		}

		var template = "\r\n\t\t\t<a href=\"%5$s\">\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\r\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"main\">\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img class=\"maincap\" src=\"%6$s\">\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t%11$s\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"bg\">\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div style=\"background-image: url( %2$s )\"><\/div>\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div style=\"background-image: url( %7$s )\"><\/div>\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div style=\"background-image: url( %8$s )\"><\/div>\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div style=\"background-image: url( %9$s )\"><\/div>\r\n\t\t\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"recommendation_reason %3$s\">\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t%4$s\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"appTitle\">\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h2>%1$s<\/h2>\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"discount_block_large\">\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t%10$s\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\r\n\t\t\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t\t\t\t\r\n\t\t\t\t\r\n\t\t\t<\/a>\r\n\t\t";
		var rec_template_curator = "\r\n\t\t\t<div>\r\n\t\t\t\t<img class=\"curator_avatar\" src=\"%1$s\">\r\n\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t\t<div>\r\n\t\t\t\t<p><strong>Recommended<\/strong> by<br><span>%2$s<\/span><\/p>\r\n\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t";
		var rec_template_developer = "\r\n\t\t\t<div>\r\n\t\t\t\t<img class=\"curator_avatar\" src=\"%1$s\">\r\n\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t\t<div>\r\n\t\t\t\t<p><strong>Developed<\/strong> by<br><span>%2$s<\/span><\/p>\r\n\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t";
		var rec_template_publisher = "\r\n\t\t\t<div>\r\n\t\t\t\t<img class=\"curator_avatar\" src=\"%1$s\">\r\n\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t\t<div>\r\n\t\t\t\t<p><strong>Published<\/strong> by<br><span>%2$s<\/span><\/p>\r\n\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t";
		var rec_template_franchise = "\r\n\t\t\t<div>\r\n\t\t\t\t<img class=\"curator_avatar\" src=\"%1$s\">\r\n\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t\t<div>\r\n\t\t\t\t<p>Part of <strong>Franchise<\/strong><br><span>%2$s<\/span><\/p>\r\n\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t";
		var rec_template_default = "\r\n\t\t\t<div>\r\n\t\t\t\t<p>%1$s<\/p>\r\n\t\t\t<\/div>\r\n\t\t";
		var live_stream_icon = "<div class=\"broadcast_live_stream_icon\">Live<\/div>";

		$J.each( rgClusterItems, function(i, rgInfo ){

			var rgParams = {};
			var reason = fnReason( rgInfo );
			if ( reason && reason.reason == 'curator' )
			{
				rgParams['curator_clanid'] = reason.curator.curator.clanid;
			}

			var rgItemData = GStoreItemData.GetCapParamsForItem( "genre_large_cluster", rgInfo, rgParams );
			if( !rgItemData )
			{
				return;
			}

			if( !rgItemData.screenshots )
				rgItemData.screenshots = [];


			var rec_template;

			if( reason && reason.reason == 'curator'  )
			{
				var curationData = reason.curator;

				rec_class = 'recommended_curator';
				rec_template = rec_template_curator.replace(/%1\$s/, GetAvatarURL( curationData.curator.avatar, '_medium' ) )
					.replace(/%2\$s/, V_EscapeHTML( curationData.curator.name ) );
			}
			else if( reason && reason.reason == 'creator_followed')
			{
				var creatorData = reason.creator; // creator are curators
				rec_class = 'recommended_curator';
				if( reason.relationship == 6 )
				{
					rec_template = rec_template_franchise;
				}
				else if( reason.relationship == 1 )
				{
					rec_template = rec_template_publisher;
				}
				else
				{
					rec_template = rec_template_developer;
				}

				rec_template = rec_template.replace(/%1\$s/, GetAvatarURL( creatorData.avatar, '_medium' ) )
					.replace(/%2\$s/, creatorData.name );
			}
			else if( reason && reason.reason == 'tags' )
			{
				rec_class = 'default';
				if( rgItemData.video )
					strReason = "<strong>Recommended<\/strong> because you watch videos tagged with";
				else if (rgItemData.software )
					strReason = "<strong>Recommended<\/strong> because you use software tagged with";
				else
					strReason = "<strong>Recommended<\/strong> because you played games tagged with";

				strReason = strReason + '<br><span class="taglist">' + reason.tags.join('')  + '</span>';
				rec_template = rec_template_default.replace(/%1\$s/, strReason );
			}
			else
			{
				var rec_class = 'default';
				var strReason = rgInfo.status_string || '';

				if( reason && !strReason )
				{
					if( reason.reason == 'concurrent')
						strReason = "Recommended because it's popular";
					else if ( reason.reason == 'top_seller' )
						strReason = "Top Seller";
					else if ( reason.reason == 'popular_new' )
						strReason = "New Release";
					else if ( reason.reason == 'featured' )
						strReason = "Now Available";
					else if ( reason.reason == 'specials' )
						strReason = "Recommended because it's on sale";

				}

				rec_template = rec_template_default.replace(/%1\$s/, strReason || '');

			}

			// Time for the mother of all replace() chains...
			var strHTML = PopulateTemplate(template,[
				rgItemData.name,
				rgItemData.screenshots[0] ? GetScreenshotURL( rgItemData.screenshots[0].appid || rgInfo.appid, rgItemData.screenshots[0].filename, '.600x338' ) : '',
				rec_class,
				rec_template,
				rgParams.href,
				( rgItemData.main_capsule !== undefined ) ? rgItemData.main_capsule : rgItemData.header,
				rgItemData.screenshots[1] ? GetScreenshotURL( rgItemData.screenshots[1].appid || rgInfo.appid, rgItemData.screenshots[1].filename, '.600x338' ) : '',
				rgItemData.screenshots[2] ? GetScreenshotURL( rgItemData.screenshots[2].appid || rgInfo.appid, rgItemData.screenshots[2].filename, '.600x338' ) : '',
				rgItemData.screenshots[3] ? GetScreenshotURL( rgItemData.screenshots[3].appid || rgInfo.appid, rgItemData.screenshots[3].filename, '.600x338' ) : '',
				rgItemData.discount_block,
				rgItemData.has_live_broadcast ? live_stream_icon : '' ]
			);
			var $elCapsule = $J(strHTML);

			$elCapsule.attr( rgParams );
			if ( i > 0 )
				$elCapsule.attr('data-manual-tracking', 1);

			$J('#genre_large_cluster .carousel_items').append( $elCapsule );
			$J('#genre_large_cluster .carousel_thumbs').append( $J('<div></div>') );
		});

		CreateFadingCarousel( $J('#genre_large_cluster'), 7, false);
	};
       </script>
      </div>
     </div>
